IAPI TOKAHAN. 

Dowanpi he waste, qa oyate owasin ekta iyowicakipi. Nakun dowanpi 
kin on Wakantanka inaunpapi kta, tuka nnkonspepi sni kinhan oiyokipi 
kte sni. Odowan wowapi kin de on Dakota dowanpi onspepi, qa iyokipija 
Wakantanka yatanpi kta uncinpi qa unkagapi. Odowan hena ota ehanna 
kagapi, tuka nakaha kaken apiunyanpi. 

Odowan ho hena unkagapi, Hecen candowankiyapi unpi waste. Qa 
nakun tuwe cin kinhan ho okihe wanji dowan kta, tuka ho itancan he ataya 
nina dowanpi kta. 

Hehan dowanpi iapi owasin iwanunyakapi, qa. hunh oiyape cin {accent) 
ho kin kicica sni ca piunyanpi ece. 

Hehan odowan owasin Wowapi Wakan tukte iyececapi he unkodepi, 
qa iwankam oehde unkowapi. 

Hehan wowapi ihanke ekta on odepi. dena unkagapi. Ho on odepi 
hee. Odowan qa woahiyaye on odepi hee. Taku iwohdakapi odowan 
kicica kta on odepi. Qa nakun odowan hena tuwe kage cin on sclonyapi 
kta hee. Hena on wowapi taku en un owasin tanyan sdonyapi kta. 



This is the fifth revision and enlargement of our Dakota Hymn Book. 
Almost at the beginning of the mission some few hymns were prepared. 
Their number has increased with the larger needs of the churches. Many 
of these hymns are the composition of the Dakotas themselves. Some of 
our tunes are also Dakota native airs. Thus this book has grown with the 
growth of the Dakota Mission, and is a token of the development of our 
Indian churches. 

We would here acknowledge the help given U3 by James E. Murray of 
Andover, Mass., who has harmonized a number of the native airs, and has 
otherwise assisted in the musical part of this work. 

We are also indebted to the following publishers and authors for the 
fr*?e use of their copyrights : Biglow & Main, J. Church & Co., Oliver Dit- 
son & Co., Philip Phillips, A. S. Barnes & Co., George E. Kingsley, Rev. D. 
E. Jones, Rev. E. P. Parker, W. G. Fischer, and A. J. Abbey. George E. 
Kingsley has also favored us with a tune (Dakota) composed specially for 
this work. 

JOHN POAGE WILLIAMSON, ) FmTO _ 
ALFRED LONGLEY RIGGS, ) 



ITANCAN TAWOCEKIYE KIN, 

THE LORD'S PRAYER Matt. 6:9 qa Luk. 11 : 2. 



Ateunyanpi Mahpiya ekta nanke cin : Nicaje wakandapi kte. Nitoki- 
conze u kte. 

Maka akan nitawacin econpi nunwe, malipiya kin ekta iyececa. 

Anpetu kin de anpetu woyute unqu miye. 

Qa waunlitanipi kin unkicicajuju miye, tona sicaya ecaunkiconpi wi- 
cunkicicajujupi iyececa. 

Nakun wowawiyutanye en unkayapi sni, tuka taku sica etanhan eun- 
hkaku miye. 

Wokiconze kin he niye nitawa, nakun wowasake kin, qa wowitan kin, 
owihanke wanica : Amen.

1. Wicacehpi tancan 
Kin de koyag waun, 

Tolian kinhan he wehnaka, 
Wankan mihdoye kta. 

Cho : Jesus u wo, u wo, 

Tancan wiconte kin, 
Wiconi e yakage kta, 
Hi wo, Jesus hi wo. 

2. Maka hemaca ce, 
Maka imacu kta, 

Micehpi kin wasake sni, 
Matakuni kte sni. — Clio.

Eqe tepica sni. 

Wakantanka Wasaka en. 
Ihdutanin kta ce. — Cho.

Heon wani wacin ; 

Wakantanka ninape on, 
Akahpe mayaton. — Cho. 

5. Hehan niite kin, 
Wanyag waun kta ce ; 

Nitowaste komdake kta, 
Wiconi kin hee. — Cho.

59. Psalm 103. 

i. Wanji cinca wicayuhe, 
Onsiwicakida ece ; 

Jehowa hececa : 
Konicipapi kin hena 
Cantowicayahnake ca, 

Cincawicayaya. 

2. Watusekseca hemaca, 
Oimacage sdonyaya ; 

Tanyan mayadukcan. 
Tuka waonsiyada on, 
"Watesdake miyecaton ; 

Piya koska waun. 



3. WawaMani tonakeca, 
Henakiya sdonya nanka, 

Micicajuju ye : 
Wiyohiyanpata tanhan, 
Wiyolipeyata hekanyan, 

Tokan ehpeya ye. 

4. Wicasta taanpetu he 
Askadan owihanke kte, 

Peji iyececa ; 
Hannanna ca icage ca, 
Wiyotanhan kasdapi qa, 

Hen an snis aye kta.

Wankan malipiya kin ekta, 
Wicanhpi qa wicanagi

Tuka wawahtani.

lye wahtani sni.

lye ohan waste wada,

Tokin he mayaqun.

Dehan iyokisin waun ; 

Jesus onsimada.

J 03« Makoce wanji akitapi. Heb. 11 : 14, 16. 

1. Heci makoce kin waste, 
Heci Wakantanka yanke ; 
Heci otonwe wan wakan, 
Heciya Jesus Itancan. 

2. Heciya conkaske suta, 
Heciya inyan wiyatpa ; 
Heci Wakantanka ite, 
Heci iyoyanpa hee. 

3. Heci wokokipe sni ye ; 
Heci wiconte sni ece ; 
Heci wicate cin kini ; 
Heci wiconi ohinni. 



4. Heci Wakan Woniya kin ; 
Heci oyate wiyuskin ; 
Heci woyute ota hin ; 
Heciya can wiconi kin. 

5. Heciya wokoyake ska; 
Heci wicasta kin waste ; 
Heciya wosice napa ; 
Heciya wowaste ece. 

6. Heciya tipi wan waste ; 
Heci oyanke ota ye ; 
Heci micante en yanka ; 
Heci tokin waun epca.

Minagi duecetu; 
Wopida wan ecatnon kin, 

He etan icidowan ; 
Iyotanyan mahpiya kin 

Iwankam Initancan ; 
Heciyatan kun yan, qa 

Maka kin amayani.

Yakpagan, deci yahi ; 
Nitancan kin woahtani 

Iyahdacin on nita. 
Oyate maka ohnaka, 

Owasin opeyeton ; 
Niwe kin he yatpapson qa 

Heciyatan wiconi.

Wieanlipi anipepi;

Epe cin de namahon qa, 

Wowidake mayuha.

122. Wakantanka ekta hde kta. Eyan. 12 : 7.

Unhdapi ye ;

Unhdapi ye.
